/**

 * @author Rusha
 */
public class getting_filename {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        String s;
        Scanner st=new Scanner(System.in);
        s=st.nextLine();
       File folder = new File(s);
      File[] listOfFiles = folder.listFiles();

    for (int i = 0; i < listOfFiles.length; i++) {
      if (listOfFiles[i].isFile()) {
        System.out.println("File " + listOfFiles[i].getName());
      } else if (listOfFiles[i].isDirectory()) {
        System.out.println("Directory " + listOfFiles[i].getName());
      }
    }
	
    }
    
}

 * @author Rusha

        String s;
        Scanner st=new Scanner(System.in);
        s=st.nextLine();
       File folder = new File(s);
      File[] listOfFiles = folder.listFiles();

    for (int i = 0; i < listOfFiles.length; i++) {
      if (listOfFiles[i].isFile()) {
        System.out.println("File " + listOfFiles[i].getName());
      } else if (listOfFiles[i].isDirectory()) {
        System.out.println("Directory " + listOfFiles[i].getName());
      }
    }
	
    }

package offline1;
import java.io.BufferedWriter;
import java.io.File;
import java.io.FileWriter;
import java.io.IOException;
import java.util.Scanner;

/**
 *
 * @author Rusha
 */
public class getting_filename {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        String s;
        Scanner st=new Scanner(System.in);
        s=st.nextLine();
       File folder = new File(s);
      File[] listOfFiles = folder.listFiles();

    for (int i = 0; i < listOfFiles.length; i++) {
      if (listOfFiles[i].isFile()) {
        System.out.println("File " + listOfFiles[i].getName());
      } else if (listOfFiles[i].isDirectory()) {
        System.out.println("Directory " + listOfFiles[i].getName());
      }
    }
	
    }
    
}

import java.io.BufferedWriter;
import java.io.File;
import java.io.FileWriter;
import java.io.IOException;
import java.util.Scanner;

/**
 *
 * @author Rusha
 */
public class getting_filename {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        String s;
        Scanner st=new Scanner(System.in);
        s=st.nextLine();
       File folder = new File(s);
      File[] listOfFiles = folder.listFiles();

    for (int i = 0; i < listOfFiles.length; i++) {
      if (listOfFiles[i].isFile()) {
        System.out.println("File " + listOfFiles[i].getName());
      } else if (listOfFiles[i].isDirectory()) {
        System.out.println("Directory " + listOfFiles[i].getName());
      }
    }
	
    }
    
}

 * @author Rusha
 */
public class getting_filename {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        String s;
        Scanner st=new Scanner(System.in);
        s=st.nextLine();
       File folder = new File(s);
      File[] listOfFiles = folder.listFiles();

    for (int i = 0; i < listOfFiles.length; i++) {
      if (listOfFiles[i].isFile()) {
        System.out.println("File " + listOfFiles[i].getName());
      } else if (listOfFiles[i].isDirectory()) {
        System.out.println("Directory " + listOfFiles[i].getName());
      }
    }
	
    }
    
}

package offline1;
import java.io.BufferedWriter;
import java.io.File;
import java.io.FileWriter;
import java.io.IOException;
import java.util.Scanner;

/**
 *
 * @author Rusha
 */
public class getting_filename {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        String s;
        Scanner st=new Scanner(System.in);
        s=st.nextLine();
       File folder = new File(s);
      File[] listOfFiles = folder.listFiles();

    for (int i = 0; i < listOfFiles.length; i++) {
      if (listOfFiles[i].isFile()) {
        System.out.println("File " + listOfFiles[i].getName());
      } else if (listOfFiles[i].isDirectory()) {
        System.out.println("Directory " + listOfFiles[i].getName());
      }
    }
	
    }

package offline1;
import java.io.BufferedWriter;
import java.io.File;
import java.io.FileWriter;
import java.io.IOException;
import java.util.Scanner;

/**
 *
 * @author Rusha
 */
public class getting_filename {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        String s;
        Scanner st=new Scanner(System.in);
        s=st.nextLine();
       File folder = new File(s);
      File[] listOfFiles = folder.listFiles();

    for (int i = 0; i < listOfFiles.length; i++) {
      if (listOfFiles[i].isFile()) {
        System.out.println("File " + listOfFiles[i].getName());
      } else if (listOfFiles[i].isDirectory()) {
        System.out.println("Directory " + listOfFiles[i].getName());
      }
    }
	
    }
    
}

import java.io.BufferedWriter;

/**
 *
 * @author Rusha
 */
public class getting_filename {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        String s;
        Scanner st=new Scanner(System.in);
        s=st.nextLine();
       File folder = new File(s);
      File[] listOfFiles = folder.listFiles();

    for (int i = 0; i < listOfFiles.length; i++) {
      if (listOfFiles[i].isFile()) {
        System.out.println("File " + listOfFiles[i].getName());
      } else if (listOfFiles[i].isDirectory()) {
        System.out.println("Directory " + listOfFiles[i].getName());
      }
    }
	
    }
    
}

import java.io.BufferedWriter;
import java.io.File;
import java.io.FileWriter;
import java.io.IOException;
import java.util.Scanner;

/**
 *
 * @author Rusha
 */
public class getting_filename {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        String s;
        Scanner st=new Scanner(System.in);
        s=st.nextLine();
       File folder = new File(s);
      File[] listOfFiles = folder.listFiles();

    for (int i = 0; i < listOfFiles.length; i++) {
      if (listOfFiles[i].isFile()) {
        System.out.println("File " + listOfFiles[i].getName());
      } else if (listOfFiles[i].isDirectory()) {
        System.out.println("Directory " + listOfFiles[i].getName());
      }
    }
	
    }
    
}

public class getting_filename {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        String s;
        Scanner st=new Scanner(System.in);
        s=st.nextLine();
       File folder = new File(s);
      File[] listOfFiles = folder.listFiles();

    for (int i = 0; i < listOfFiles.length; i++) {
      if (listOfFiles[i].isFile()) {
        System.out.println("File " + listOfFiles[i].getName());
      } else if (listOfFiles[i].isDirectory()) {
        System.out.println("Directory " + listOfFiles[i].getName());
      }
    }
	
    }
    
}
    } else if (listOfFiles[i].isDirectory()) {

package offline1;
import java.io.BufferedWriter;
import java.io.File;
import java.io.FileWriter;
import java.io.IOException;
import java.util.Scanner;

/**
 *
 * @author Rusha
 */
public class getting_filename {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        String s;
        Scanner st=new Scanner(System.in);
        s=st.nextLine();
       File folder = new File(s);
      File[] listOfFiles = folder.listFiles();

    for (int i = 0; i < listOfFiles.length; i++) {
      if (listOfFiles[i].isFile()) {
        System.out.println("File " + listOfFiles[i].getName());
      } else if (listOfFiles[i].isDirectory()) {
        System.out.println("Directory " + listOfFiles[i].getName());
      }
    }
	
    }
    
}

       File folder = new File(s);
      File[] listOfFiles = folder.listFiles();

    for (int i = 0; i < listOfFiles.length; i++) {
      if (listOfFiles[i].isFile()) {
        System.out.println("File " + listOfFiles[i].getName());
      } else if (listOfFiles[i].isDirectory()) {
        System.out.println("Directory " + listOfFiles[i].getName());
      }
    }
	
    }

package offline1;
import java.io.BufferedWriter;
import java.io.File;
import java.io.FileWriter;
import java.io.IOException;
import java.util.Scanner;

/**
 *
 * @author Rusha
 */
public class getting_filename {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        String s;
        Scanner st=new Scanner(System.in);
        s=st.nextLine();
       File folder = new File(s);
      File[] listOfFiles = folder.listFiles();

    for (int i = 0; i < listOfFiles.length; i++) {
      if (listOfFiles[i].isFile()) {
        System.out.println("File " + listOfFiles[i].getName());
      } else if (listOfFiles[i].isDirectory()) {
        System.out.println("Directory " + listOfFiles[i].getName());
      }
    }
	
    }
    
}

import java.io.FileWriter;
import java.io.IOException;
import java.util.Scanner;

/**
 *
 * @author Rusha
 */
public class getting_filename {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        String s;
        Scanner st=new Scanner(System.in);
        s=st.nextLine();
       File folder = new File(s);
      File[] listOfFiles = folder.listFiles();

    for (int i = 0; i < listOfFiles.length; i++) {
      if (listOfFiles[i].isFile()) {
        System.out.println("File " + listOfFiles[i].getName());
      } else if (listOfFiles[i].isDirectory()) {
        System.out.println("Directory " + listOfFiles[i].getName());
      }
    }
	
    }
    
}
    } else if (listOfFiles[i].isDirectory()) {

package offline1;
import java.io.BufferedWriter;
import java.io.File;
import java.io.FileWriter;
import java.io.IOException;
import java.util.Scanner;

/**
 *
 * @author Rusha
 */
public class getting_filename {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        String s;
        Scanner st=new Scanner(System.in);
        s=st.nextLine();
       File folder = new File(s);
      File[] listOfFiles = folder.listFiles();

    for (int i = 0; i < listOfFiles.length; i++) {
      if (listOfFiles[i].isFile()) {
        System.out.println("File " + listOfFiles[i].getName());

import java.io.FileWriter;
import java.io.IOException;
import java.util.Scanner;

/**
 *
 * @author Rusha
 */
public class getting_filename {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        String s;
        Scanner st=new Scanner(System.in);
        s=st.nextLine();
       File folder = new File(s);
      File[] listOfFiles = folder.listFiles();

    for (int i = 0; i < listOfFiles.length; i++) {
      if (listOfFiles[i].isFile()) {
        System.out.println("File " + listOfFiles[i].getName());
      } else if (listOfFiles[i].isDirectory()) {
        System.out.println("Directory " + listOfFiles[i].getName());
      }
    }
	
    }
    
}

package offline1;
import java.io.BufferedWriter;
import java.io.File;
import java.io.FileWriter;
import java.io.IOException;
import java.util.Scanner;

/**
 *
 * @author Rusha
 */
public class getting_filename {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        String s;
        Scanner st=new Scanner(System.in);
        s=st.nextLine();
       File folder = new File(s);
      File[] listOfFiles = folder.listFiles();

    for (int i = 0; i < listOfFiles.length; i++) {
      if (listOfFiles[i].isFile()) {
        System.out.println("File " + listOfFiles[i].getName());
      } else if (listOfFiles[i].isDirectory()) {
        System.out.println("Directory " + listOfFiles[i].getName());
      }
    }

package offline1;
import java.io.BufferedWriter;
import java.io.File;
import java.io.FileWriter;
import java.io.IOException;
import java.util.Scanner;

/**
 *
 * @author Rusha
 */
public class getting_filename {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        String s;
        Scanner st=new Scanner(System.in);
        s=st.nextLine();
       File folder = new File(s);
      File[] listOfFiles = folder.listFiles();

    for (int i = 0; i < listOfFiles.length; i++) {
      if (listOfFiles[i].isFile()) {
        System.out.println("File " + listOfFiles[i].getName());
      } else if (listOfFiles[i].isDirectory()) {
        System.out.println("Directory " + listOfFiles[i].getName());
      }
    }
	
    }
    
}
    } else if (listOfFiles[i].isDirectory()) {

      File[] listOfFiles = folder.listFiles();

        System.out.println("File " + listOfFiles[i].getName());
      } else if (listOfFiles[i].isDirectory()) {

package offline1;
import java.io.BufferedWriter;
import java.io.File;
import java.io.FileWriter;
import java.io.IOException;
import java.util.Scanner;

/**
 *
 * @author Rusha
 */
public class getting_filename {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        String s;
        Scanner st=new Scanner(System.in);
        s=st.nextLine();
       File folder = new File(s);
      File[] listOfFiles = folder.listFiles();

    for (int i = 0; i < listOfFiles.length; i++) {
      if (listOfFiles[i].isFile()) {
        System.out.println("File " + listOfFiles[i].getName());
      } else if (listOfFiles[i].isDirectory()) {
        System.out.println("Directory " + listOfFiles[i].getName());
      }
    }
	
    }
    
}

        s=st.nextLine();
       File folder = new File(s);

        System.out.println("File " + listOfFiles[i].getName());
      } else if (listOfFiles[i].isDirectory()) {

        System.out.println("File " + listOfFiles[i].getName());
      } else if (listOfFiles[i].isDirectory()) {

      }
    }

import java.io.FileWriter;
import java.io.IOException;
import java.util.Scanner;

/**
 *
 * @author Rusha
 */
public class getting_filename {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        String s;
        Scanner st=new Scanner(System.in);
        s=st.nextLine();
       File folder = new File(s);
      File[] listOfFiles = folder.listFiles();

    for (int i = 0; i < listOfFiles.length; i++) {
      if (listOfFiles[i].isFile()) {
        System.out.println("File " + listOfFiles[i].getName());
      } else if (listOfFiles[i].isDirectory()) {
        System.out.println("Directory " + listOfFiles[i].getName());
      }
    }
	
    }
    
}

package offline1;
import java.io.BufferedWriter;
import java.io.File;
import java.io.FileWriter;
import java.io.IOException;
import java.util.Scanner;

/**
 *
 * @author Rusha
 */
public class getting_filename {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        String s;
        Scanner st=new Scanner(System.in);
        s=st.nextLine();
       File folder = new File(s);
      File[] listOfFiles = folder.listFiles();

    for (int i = 0; i < listOfFiles.length; i++) {
      if (listOfFiles[i].isFile()) {
        System.out.println("File " + listOfFiles[i].getName());
      } else if (listOfFiles[i].isDirectory()) {
        System.out.println("Directory " + listOfFiles[i].getName());
      }
    }

import java.io.FileWriter;
import java.io.IOException;
import java.util.Scanner;

/**
 *
 * @author Rusha
 */
public class getting_filename {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        String s;
        Scanner st=new Scanner(System.in);
        s=st.nextLine();
       File folder = new File(s);
      File[] listOfFiles = folder.listFiles();

    for (int i = 0; i < listOfFiles.length; i++) {
      if (listOfFiles[i].isFile()) {
        System.out.println("File " + listOfFiles[i].getName());
      } else if (listOfFiles[i].isDirectory()) {
        System.out.println("Directory " + listOfFiles[i].getName());
      }
    }
	
    }
    
}

import java.io.BufferedWriter;
import java.io.File;
import java.io.FileWriter;
import java.io.IOException;
import java.util.Scanner;

/**
 *
 * @author Rusha
 */
public class getting_filename {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        String s;
        Scanner st=new Scanner(System.in);
        s=st.nextLine();
       File folder = new File(s);
      File[] listOfFiles = folder.listFiles();

    for (int i = 0; i < listOfFiles.length; i++) {
      if (listOfFiles[i].isFile()) {
        System.out.println("File " + listOfFiles[i].getName());
      } else if (listOfFiles[i].isDirectory()) {

      }
    }

package offline1;
import java.io.BufferedWriter;
import java.io.File;
import java.io.FileWriter;
import java.io.IOException;
import java.util.Scanner;

/**
 *
 * @author Rusha
 */
public class getting_filename {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        String s;
        Scanner st=new Scanner(System.in);
        s=st.nextLine();
       File folder = new File(s);
      File[] listOfFiles = folder.listFiles();

    for (int i = 0; i < listOfFiles.length; i++) {
      if (listOfFiles[i].isFile()) {
        System.out.println("File " + listOfFiles[i].getName());
      } else if (listOfFiles[i].isDirectory()) {
        System.out.println("Directory " + listOfFiles[i].getName());
      }
    }
	
    }
    
}

        System.out.println("File " + listOfFiles[i].getName());
      } else if (listOfFiles[i].isDirectory()) {

      }

package offline1;
import java.io.BufferedWriter;
import java.io.File;
import java.io.FileWriter;
import java.io.IOException;
import java.util.Scanner;

/**
 *
 * @author Rusha
 */
public class getting_filename {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        String s;
        Scanner st=new Scanner(System.in);
        s=st.nextLine();
       File folder = new File(s);
      File[] listOfFiles = folder.listFiles();

    for (int i = 0; i < listOfFiles.length; i++) {
      if (listOfFiles[i].isFile()) {
        System.out.println("File " + listOfFiles[i].getName());
      } else if (listOfFiles[i].isDirectory()) {
        System.out.println("Directory " + listOfFiles[i].getName());
      }
    }
	
    }
    
}

import java.io.IOException;
import java.util.Scanner;

/**
 *
 * @author Rusha
 */
public class getting_filename {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        String s;
        Scanner st=new Scanner(System.in);
        s=st.nextLine();
       File folder = new File(s);
      File[] listOfFiles = folder.listFiles();

    for (int i = 0; i < listOfFiles.length; i++) {
      if (listOfFiles[i].isFile()) {
        System.out.println("File " + listOfFiles[i].getName());
      } else if (listOfFiles[i].isDirectory()) {
        System.out.println("Directory " + listOfFiles[i].getName());
      }
    }
	
    }
    
}

package offline1;
import java.io.BufferedWriter;
import java.io.File;
import java.io.FileWriter;
import java.io.IOException;
import java.util.Scanner;

/**
 *
 * @author Rusha
 */
public class getting_filename {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        String s;
        Scanner st=new Scanner(System.in);
        s=st.nextLine();
       File folder = new File(s);
      File[] listOfFiles = folder.listFiles();

    for (int i = 0; i < listOfFiles.length; i++) {
      if (listOfFiles[i].isFile()) {
        System.out.println("File " + listOfFiles[i].getName());
      } else if (listOfFiles[i].isDirectory()) {
        System.out.println("Directory " + listOfFiles[i].getName());
      }
    }
	
    }
    
}

package offline1;
import java.io.BufferedWriter;
import java.io.File;
import java.io.FileWriter;
import java.io.IOException;
import java.util.Scanner;

/**
 *
 * @author Rusha
 */
public class getting_filename {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        String s;
        Scanner st=new Scanner(System.in);
        s=st.nextLine();
       File folder = new File(s);
      File[] listOfFiles = folder.listFiles();

    for (int i = 0; i < listOfFiles.length; i++) {
      if (listOfFiles[i].isFile()) {
        System.out.println("File " + listOfFiles[i].getName());
      } else if (listOfFiles[i].isDirectory()) {
        System.out.println("Directory " + listOfFiles[i].getName());
      }
    }
	
    }
    
}
